this.retryBackoff = new ExponentialBackoff(retryBackoffMs,\n   136→                CommonClientConfigs.RETRY_BACKOFF_EXP_BASE,\n   137→                retryBackoffMaxMs,\n   138→                CommonClientConfigs.RETRY_BACKOFF_JITTER);\n   139→        this.deliveryTimeoutMs = deliveryTimeoutMs;\n   140→        this.enableAdaptivePartitioning = partitionerConfig.enableAdaptivePartitioning;\n   141→        this.partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs = partitionerConfig.partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs;\n   142→        this.free = bufferPool;\n   143→        this.incomplete = new IncompleteBatches();\n   144→        this.muted = new HashSet<>();\n   145→        this.time = time;\n   146→        nodesDrainIndex = new HashMap<>();\n   147→        this.transactionManager = transactionManager;\n   148→        registerMetrics(metrics, metricGrpName);\n   149→    }\n   150→\n   151→    /**\n   152→     * Create a new record accumulator with default partitioner config\n   153→     *\n   154→     * @param logContext The log context used for logging\n   155→     * @param batchSize The size to use when allocating {@link MemoryRecords} instances\n   156→     * @param compression The compression codec for the records\n   157→     * @param lingerMs An artificial delay time to add before declaring a records instance that isn't full ready for\n   158→     *        sending. This allows time for more records to arrive. Setting a non-zero lingerMs will trade off some\n   159→     *        latency for potentially better throughput due to more batching (and hence fewer, larger requests).\n   160→     * @param retryBackoffMs An artificial delay time to retry the produce request upon receiving an error. This avoids\n   161→     *        exhausting all retries in a short period of time.\n   162→     * @param retryBackoffMaxMs The upper bound of the retry backoff time.\n   163→     * @param deliveryTimeoutMs An upper bound on the time to report success or failure on record delivery\n   164→     * @param metrics The metrics\n   165→     * @param metricGrpName The metric group name\n   166→     * @param time The time instance to use\n   167→     * @param transactionManager The shared transaction state object which tracks producer IDs, epochs, and sequence\n   168→     *                           numbers per partition.\n   169→     * @param bufferPool The buffer pool\n   170→     */\n   171→    public RecordAccumulator(LogContext logContext,\n   172→                             int batchSize,\n   173→                             Compression compression,\n   174→                             int lingerMs,\n   175→                             long retryBackoffMs,\n   176→                             long retryBackoffMaxMs,\n   177→                             int deliveryTimeoutMs,\n   178→                             Metrics metrics,\n   179→                             String metricGrpName,\n   180→                             Time time,\n   181→                             TransactionManager transactionManager,\n   182→                             BufferPool bufferPool) {\n   183→        this(logContext,\n   184→            batchSize,\n   185→            compression,\n   186→            lingerMs,\n   187→            retryBackoffMs,\n   188→            retryBackoffMaxMs,\n   189→            deliveryTimeoutMs,\n   190→            new PartitionerConfig(),\n   191→            metrics,\n   192→            metricGrpName,\n   193→            time,\n   194→            transactionManager,\n   195→            bufferPool);\n   196→    }\n   197→\n   198→    private void registerMetrics(Metrics metrics, String metricGrpName) {\n   199→        metrics.addMetric(\n   200→            metrics.metricName(\"waiting-threads\", metricGrpName,\n   201→                \"The number of user threads blocked waiting for buffer memory to enqueue their records\"),\n   202→            (config, now) -> free.queued());\n   203→\n   204→        metrics.addMetric(\n   205→            metrics.metricName(\"buffer-total-bytes\", metricGrpName,\n   206→                \"The maximum amount of buffer memory the client can use (whether or not it is currently used).\"),\n   207→            (config, now) -> free.totalMemory());\n   208→\n   209→        metrics.addMetric(\n   210→            metrics.metricName(\"buffer-available-bytes\", metricGrpName,\n   211→                \"The total amount of buffer memory that is not being used (either unallocated or in the free list).\"),\n   212→            (config, now) -> free.availableMemory());\n   213→    }\n   214→\n   215→    private void setPartition(AppendCallbacks callbacks, int partition) {\n   216→        if (callbacks != null)\n   217→            callbacks.setPartition(partition);\n   218→    }\n   219→\n   220→    /**\n   221→     * Check if partition concurrently changed, or we need to complete previously disabled partition change.\n   222→     *\n   223→     * @param topic The topic\n   224→     * @param topicInfo The topic info\n   225→     * @param partitionInfo The built-in partitioner's partition info\n   226→     * @param deque The partition queue\n   227→     * @param nowMs The current time, in milliseconds\n   228→     * @param cluster THe cluster metadata\n   229→     * @return 'true' if partition changed and we need to get new partition info and retry,\n   230→     *         'false' otherwise\n   231→     */\n   232→    private boolean partitionChanged(String topic,\n   233→                                     TopicInfo topicInfo,\n   234→                                     BuiltInPartitioner.StickyPartitionInfo partitionInfo,\n   235→                                     Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, long nowMs,\n   236→                                     Cluster cluster) {\n   237→        if (topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.isPartitionChanged(partitionInfo)) {\n   238→            log.trace(\"Partition {} for topic {} switched by a concurrent append, retrying\",\n   239→                    partitionInfo.partition(), topic);\n   240→            return true;\n   241→        }\n   242→\n   243→        // We might have disabled partition switch if the queue had incomplete batches.\n   244→        // Check if all batches are full now and switch .\n   245→        if (allBatchesFull(deque)) {\n   246→            topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, 0, cluster, true);\n   247→            if (topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.isPartitionChanged(partitionInfo)) {\n   248→                log.trace(\"Completed previously disabled switch for topic {} partition {}, retrying\",\n   249→                        topic, partitionInfo.partition());\n   250→                return true;\n   251→            }\n   252→        }\n   253→\n   254→        return false;\n   255→    }\n   256→\n   257→    /**\n   258→     * Add a record to the accumulator, return the append result\n   259→     * <p>\n   260→     * The append result will contain the future metadata, and flag for whether the appended batch is full or a new batch is created\n   261→     * <p>\n   262→     *\n   263→     * @param topic The topic to which this record is being sent\n   264→     * @param partition The partition to which this record is being sent or RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION\n   265→     *                  if any partition could be used\n   266→     * @param timestamp The timestamp of the record\n   267→     * @param key The key for the record\n   268→     * @param value The value for the record\n   269→     * @param headers the Headers for the record\n   270→     * @param callbacks The callbacks to execute\n   271→     * @param maxTimeToBlock The maximum time in milliseconds to block for buffer memory to be available\n   272→     * @param nowMs The current time, in milliseconds\n   273→     * @param cluster The cluster metadata\n   274→     */\n   275→    public RecordAppendResult append(String topic,\n   276→                                     int partition,\n   277→                                     long timestamp,\n   278→                                     byte[] key,\n   279→                                     byte[] value,\n   280→                                     Header[] headers,\n   281→                                     AppendCallbacks callbacks,\n   282→                                     long maxTimeToBlock,\n   283→                                     long nowMs,\n   284→                                     Cluster cluster) throws InterruptedException {\n   285→        TopicInfo topicInfo = topicInfoMap.computeIfAbsent(topic, k -> new TopicInfo(createBuiltInPartitioner(logContext, k, batchSize)));\n   286→\n   287→        // We keep track of the number of appending thread to make sure we do not miss batches in\n   288→        // abortIncompleteBatches().\n   289→        appendsInProgress.incrementAndGet();\n   290→        ByteBuffer buffer = null;\n   291→        if (headers == null) headers = Record.EMPTY_HEADERS;\n   292→        try {\n   293→            // Loop to retry in case we encounter partitioner's race conditions.\n   294→            while (true) {\n   295→                // If the message doesn't have any partition affinity, so we pick a partition based on the broker\n   296→                // availability and performance.  Note, that here we peek current partition before we hold the\n   297→                // deque lock, so we'll need to make sure that it's not changed while we were waiting for the\n   298→                // deque lock.\n   299→                final BuiltInPartitioner.StickyPartitionInfo partitionInfo;\n   300→                final int effectivePartition;\n   301→                if (partition == RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION) {\n   302→                    partitionInfo = topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.peekCurrentPartitionInfo(cluster);\n   303→                    effectivePartition = partitionInfo.partition();\n   304→                } else {\n   305→                    partitionInfo = null;\n   306→                    effectivePartition = partition;\n   307→                }\n   308→\n   309→                // Now that we know the effective partition, let the caller know.\n   310→                setPartition(callbacks, effectivePartition);\n   311→\n   312→                // check if we have an in-progress batch\n   313→                Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = topicInfo.batches.computeIfAbsent(effectivePartition, k -> new ArrayDeque<>());\n   314→                synchronized (dq) {\n   315→                    // After taking the lock, validate that the partition hasn't changed and retry.\n   316→                    if (partitionChanged(topic, topicInfo, partitionInfo, dq, nowMs, cluster))\n   317→                        continue;\n   318→\n   319→                    RecordAppendResult appendResult = tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, dq, nowMs);\n   320→                    if (appendResult != null) {\n   321→                        // If queue has incomplete batches we disable switch (see comments in updatePartitionInfo).\n   322→                        boolean enableSwitch = allBatchesFull(dq);\n   323→                        topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, appendResult.appendedBytes, cluster, enableSwitch);\n   324→                        return appendResult;\n   325→                    }\n   326→                }\n   327→\n   328→                if (buffer == null) {\n   329→                    int size = Math.max(this.batchSize, AbstractRecords.estimateSizeInBytesUpperBound(\n   330→                            RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression.type(), key, value, headers));\n   331→                    log.trace(\"Allocating a new {} byte message buffer for topic {} partition {} with remaining timeout {}ms\", size, topic, effectivePartition, maxTimeToBlock);\n   332→                    // This call may block if we exhausted buffer space.\n   333→                    buffer = free.allocate(size, maxTimeToBlock);\n   334→                    // Update the current time in case the buffer allocation blocked above.\n   335→                    // NOTE: getting time may be expensive, so calling it under a lock\n   336→                    // should be avoided.\n   337→                    nowMs = time.milliseconds();\n   338→                }\n   339→\n   340→                synchronized (dq) {\n   341→                    // After taking the lock, validate that the partition hasn't changed and retry.\n   342→                    if (partitionChanged(topic, topicInfo, partitionInfo, dq, nowMs, cluster))\n   343→                        continue;\n   344→\n   345→                    RecordAppendResult appendResult = appendNewBatch(topic, effectivePartition, dq, timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, buffer, nowMs);\n   346→                    // Set buffer to null, so that deallocate doesn't return it back to free pool, since it's used in the batch.\n   347→                    if (appendResult.newBatchCreated)\n   348→                        buffer = null;\n   349→                    // If queue has incomplete batches we disable switch (see comments in updatePartitionInfo).\n   350→                    boolean enableSwitch = allBatchesFull(dq);\n   351→                    topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, appendResult.appendedBytes, cluster, enableSwitch);\n   352→                    return appendResult;\n   353→                }\n   354→            }\n   355→        } finally {\n   356→            free.deallocate(buffer);\n   357→            appendsInProgress.decrementAndGet();\n   358→        }\n   359→    }\n   360→\n   361→    /**\n   362→     * Append a new batch to the queue\n   363→     *\n   364→     * @param topic The topic\n   365→     * @param partition The partition (cannot be RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION)\n   366→     * @param dq The queue\n   367→     * @param timestamp The timestamp of the record\n   368→     * @param key The key for the record\n   369→     * @param value The value for the record\n   370→     * @param headers the Headers for the record\n   371→     * @param callbacks The callbacks to execute\n   372→     * @param buffer The buffer for the new batch\n   373→     * @param nowMs The current time, in milliseconds\n   374→     */\n   375→    private RecordAppendResult appendNewBatch(String topic,\n   376→                                              int partition,\n   377→                                              Deque<ProducerBatch> dq,\n   378→                                              long timestamp,\n   379→                                              byte[] key,\n   380→                                              byte[] value,\n   381→                                              Header[] headers,\n   382→                                              AppendCallbacks callbacks,\n   383→                                              ByteBuffer buffer,\n   384→                                              long nowMs) {\n   385→        assert partition != RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION;\n   386→\n   387→        RecordAppendResult appendResult = tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, dq, nowMs);\n   388→        if (appendResult != null) {\n   389→            // Somebody else found us a batch, return the one we waited for! Hopefully this doesn't happen often...\n   390→            return appendResult;\n   391→        }\n   392→\n   393→        MemoryRecordsBuilder recordsBuilder = recordsBuilder(buffer);\n   394→        ProducerBatch batch = new ProducerBatch(new TopicPartition(topic, partition), recordsBuilder, nowMs);\n   395→        FutureRecordMetadata future = Objects.requireNonNull(batch.tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers,\n   396→                callbacks, nowMs));\n   397→\n   398→        dq.addLast(batch);\n   399→        incomplete.add(batch);\n   400→\n   401→        return new RecordAppendResult(future, dq.size() > 1 || batch.isFull(), true, batch.estimatedSizeInBytes());\n   402→    }\n   403→\n   404→    private MemoryRecordsBuilder recordsBuilder(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n   405→        return MemoryRecords.builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, 0L);\n   406→    }\n   407→\n   408→    /**\n   409→     * Check if all batches in the queue are full.\n   410→     */\n   411→    private boolean allBatchesFull(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque) {\n   412→        // Only the last batch may be incomplete, so we just check that.\n   413→        ProducerBatch last = deque.peekLast();\n   414→        return last == null || last.isFull();\n   415→    }\n   416→\n   417→     /**\n   418→     *  Try to append to a ProducerBatch.\n   419→     *\n   420→     *  If it is full, we return null and a new batch is created. We also close the batch for record appends to free up\n   421→     *  resources like compression buffers. The batch will be fully closed (ie. the record batch headers will be written\n   422→     *  and memory records built) in one of the following cases (whichever comes first): right before send,\n   423→     *  if it is expired, or when the producer is closed.\n   424→     */\n   425→    private RecordAppendResult tryAppend(long timestamp, byte[] key, byte[] value, Header[] headers,\n   426→                                         Callback callback, Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, long nowMs) {\n   427→        if (closed)\n   428→            throw new KafkaException(\"Producer closed while send in progress\");\n   429→        ProducerBatch last = deque.peekLast();\n   430→        if (last != null) {\n   431→            int initialBytes = last.estimatedSizeInBytes();\n   432→            FutureRecordMetadata future = last.tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callback, nowMs);\n   433→            if (future == null) {\n   434→                last.closeForRecordAppends();\n   435→            } else {\n   436→                int appendedBytes = last.estimatedSizeInBytes() - initialBytes;\n   437→                return new RecordAppendResult(future, deque.size() > 1 || last.isFull(), false, appendedBytes);\n   438→            }\n   439→        }\n   440→        return null;\n   441→    }\n   442→\n   443→    private boolean isMuted(TopicPartition tp) {\n   444→        return muted.contains(tp);\n   445→    }\n   446→\n   447→    public void resetNextBatchExpiryTime() {\n   448→        nextBatchExpiryTimeMs = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n   449→    }\n   450→\n   451→    public void maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(ProducerBatch batch) {\n   452→        if (batch.createdMs + deliveryTimeoutMs  > 0) {\n   453→            // the non-negative check is to guard us against potential overflow due to setting\n   454→            // a large value for deliveryTimeoutMs\n   455→            nextBatchExpiryTimeMs = Math.min(nextBatchExpiryTimeMs, batch.createdMs + deliveryTimeoutMs);\n   456→        } else {\n   457→            log.warn(\"Skipping next batch expiry time update due to addition overflow: \"\n   458→                + \"batch.createMs={}, deliveryTimeoutMs={}\", batch.createdMs, deliveryTimeoutMs);\n   459→        }\n   460→    }\n   461→\n   462→    /**\n   463→     * Get a list of batches which have been sitting in the accumulator too long and need to be expired.\n   464→     */\n   465→    public List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches(long now) {\n   466→        List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = new ArrayList<>();\n   467→        for (TopicInfo topicInfo : topicInfoMap.values()) {\n   468→            for (Deque<ProducerBatch> deque : topicInfo.batches.values()) {\n   469→                // expire the batches in the order of sending\n   470→                synchronized (deque) {\n   471→                    while (!deque.isEmpty()) {\n   472→                        ProducerBatch batch = deque.getFirst();\n   473→                        if (batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(deliveryTimeoutMs, now)) {\n   474→                            deque.poll();\n   475→                            batch.abortRecordAppends();\n   476→                            expiredBatches.add(batch);\n   477→                        } else {\n   478→                            maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(batch);\n   479→                            break;\n   480→                        }\n   481→                    }\n   482→                }\n   483→            }\n   484→        }\n   485→        return expiredBatches;\n   486→    }\n   487→\n   488→    public long getDeliveryTimeoutMs() {\n   489→        return deliveryTimeoutMs;\n   490→    }\n   491→\n   492→    /**\n   493→     * Re-enqueue the given record batch in the accumulator. In Sender.completeBatch method, we check\n   494→     * whether the batch has reached deliveryTimeoutMs or not. Hence we do not do the delivery timeout check here.\n   495→     */\n   496→    public void reenqueue(ProducerBatch batch, long now) {\n   497→        batch.reenqueued(now);\n   498→        Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = getOrCreateDeque(batch.topicPartition);\n   499→        synchronized (deque) {\n   500→            if (transactionManager != null)\n   501→                insertInSequenceOrder(deque, batch);\n   502→            else\n   503→                deque.addFirst(batch);\n   504→        }\n   505→    }\n   506→\n   507→    /**\n   508→     * Split the big batch that has been rejected and reenqueue the split batches in to the accumulator.\n   509→     * @return the number of split batches.\n   510→     */\n   511→    public int splitAndReenqueue(ProducerBatch bigBatch) {\n   512→        // Reset the estimated compression ratio to the initial value or the big batch compression ratio, whichever\n   513→        // is bigger. There are several different ways to do the reset. We chose the most conservative one to ensure\n   514→        // the split doesn't happen too often.\n   515→        CompressionRatioEstimator.setEstimation(bigBatch.topicPartition.topic(), compression.type(),\n   516→                                                Math.max(1.0f, (float) bigBatch.compressionRatio()));\n   517→        Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = bigBatch.split(this.batchSize);\n   518→        int numSplitBatches = dq.size();\n   519→        Deque<ProducerBatch> partitionDequeue = getOrCreateDeque(bigBatch.topicPartition);\n   520→        while (!dq.isEmpty()) {\n   521→            ProducerBatch batch = dq.pollLast();\n   522→            incomplete.add(batch);\n   523→            // We treat the newly split batches as if they are not even tried.\n   524→            synchronized (partitionDequeue) {\n   525→                if (transactionManager != null) {\n   526→                    // We should track the newly created batches since they already have assigned sequences.\n   527→                    transactionManager.addInFlightBatch(batch);\n   528→                    insertInSequenceOrder(partitionDequeue, batch);\n   529→                } else {\n   530→                    partitionDequeue.addFirst(batch);\n   531→                }\n   532→            }\n   533→        }\n   534→        return numSplitBatches;\n   535→    }\n   536→\n   537→    // We will have to do extra work to ensure the queue is in order when requests are being retried and there are\n   538→    // multiple requests in flight to that partition. If the first in flight request fails to append, then all the\n   539→    // subsequent in flight requests will also fail because the sequence numbers will not be accepted.\n   540→    //\n   541→    // Further, once batches are being retried, we are reduced to a single in flight request for that partition. So when\n   542→    // the subsequent batches come back in sequence order, they will have to be placed further back in the queue.\n   543→    //\n   544→    // Note that this assumes that all the batches in the queue which have an assigned sequence also have the current\n   545→    // producer id. We will not attempt to reorder messages if the producer id has changed, we will throw an\n   546→    // IllegalStateException instead.\n   547→    private void insertInSequenceOrder(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, ProducerBatch batch) {\n   548→        // When we are re-enqueueing and have enabled idempotence, the re-enqueued batch must always have a sequence.\n   549→        if (batch.baseSequence() == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n   550→            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Trying to re-enqueue a batch which doesn't have a sequence even \" +\n   551→                \"though idempotency is enabled.\");\n   552→\n   553→        if (!transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(batch.topicPartition))\n   554→            throw new IllegalStateException(\"We are re-enqueueing a batch which is not tracked as part of the in flight \" +\n   555→                \"requests. batch.topicPartition: \" + batch.topicPartition + \"; batch.baseSequence: \" + batch.baseSequence());\n   556→\n   557→        ProducerBatch firstBatchInQueue = deque.peekFirst();\n   558→        if (firstBatchInQueue != null && firstBatchInQueue.hasSequence() && firstBatchInQueue.baseSequence() < batch.baseSequence()) {\n   559→            // The incoming batch can't be inserted at the front of the queue without violating the sequence ordering.\n   560→            // This means that the incoming batch should be placed somewhere further back.\n   561→            // We need to find the right place for the incoming batch and insert it there.\n   562→            // We will only enter this branch if we have multiple inflights sent to different brokers and we need to retry\n   563→            // the inflight batches.\n   564→            //\n   565→            // Since we reenqueue exactly one batch a time and ensure that the queue is ordered by sequence always, it\n   566→            // is a simple linear scan of a subset of the in flight batches to find the right place in the queue each time.\n   567→            List<ProducerBatch> orderedBatches = new ArrayList<>();\n   568→            while (deque.peekFirst() != null && deque.peekFirst().hasSequence() && deque.peekFirst().baseSequence() < batch.baseSequence())\n   569→                orderedBatches.add(deque.pollFirst());\n   570→\n   571→            log.debug(\"Reordered incoming batch with sequence {} for partition {}. It was placed in the queue at \" +\n   572→                \"position {}\", batch.baseSequence(), batch.topicPartition, orderedBatches.size());\n   573→            // Either we have reached a point where there are batches without a sequence (ie. never been drained\n   574→            // and are hence in order by default), or the batch at the front of the queue has a sequence greater\n   575→            // than the incoming batch. This is the right place to add the incoming batch.\n   576→            deque.addFirst(batch);\n   577→\n   578→            // Now we have to re insert the previously queued batches in the right order.\n   579→            for (int i = orderedBatches.size() - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n   580→                deque.addFirst(orderedBatches.get(i));\n   581→            }\n   582→\n   583→            // At this point, the incoming batch has been queued in the correct place according to its sequence.\n   584→        } else {\n   585→            deque.addFirst(batch);\n   586→        }\n   587→    }\n   588→\n   589→    /**\n   590→     * Add the leader to the ready nodes if the batch is ready\n   591→     *\n   592→     * @param exhausted 'true' is the buffer pool is exhausted\n   593→     * @param part The partition\n   594→     * @param leader The leader for the partition\n   595→     * @param waitedTimeMs How long batch waited\n   596→     * @param backingOff Is backing off\n   597→     * @param backoffAttempts Number of attempts for calculating backoff delay\n   598→     * @param full Is batch full\n   599→     * @param nextReadyCheckDelayMs The delay for next check\n   600→     * @param readyNodes The set of ready nodes (to be filled in)\n   601→     * @return The delay for next check\n   602→     */\n   603→    private long batchReady(boolean exhausted, TopicPartition part, Node leader,\n   604→                            long waitedTimeMs, boolean backingOff, int backoffAttempts,\n   605→                            boolean full, long nextReadyCheckDelayMs, Set<Node> readyNodes) {\n   606→        if (!readyNodes.contains(leader) && !isMuted(part)) {\n   607→            long timeToWaitMs = backingOff ? retryBackoff.backoff(backoffAttempts > 0 ? backoffAttempts - 1 : 0) : lingerMs;\n   608→            boolean expired = waitedTimeMs >= timeToWaitMs;\n   609→            boolean transactionCompleting = transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isCompleting();\n   610→            boolean sendable = full\n   611→                    || expired\n   612→                    || exhausted\n   613→                    || closed\n   614→                    || flushInProgress()\n   615→                    || transactionCompleting;\n   616→            if (sendable && !backingOff) {\n   617→                readyNodes.add(leader);\n   618→            } else {\n   619→                long timeLeftMs = Math.max(timeToWaitMs - waitedTimeMs, 0);\n   620→                // Note that this results in a conservative estimate since an un-sendable partition may have\n   621→                // a leader that will later be found to have sendable data. However, this is good enough\n   622→                // since we'll just wake up and then sleep again for the remaining time.\n   623→                nextReadyCheckDelayMs = Math.min(timeLeftMs, nextReadyCheckDelayMs);\n   624→            }\n   625→        }\n   626→        return nextReadyCheckDelayMs;\n   627→    }\n   628→\n   629→    /**\n   630→     * Iterate over partitions to see which one have batches ready and collect leaders of those\n   631→     * partitions into the set of ready nodes.  If partition has no leader, add the topic to the set\n   632→     * of topics with no leader.  This function also calculates stats for adaptive partitioning.\n   633→     *\n   634→     * @param metadataSnapshot      The cluster metadata\n   635→     * @param nowMs                 The current time\n   636→     * @param topic                 The topic\n   637→     * @param topicInfo             The topic info\n   638→     * @param nextReadyCheckDelayMs The delay for next check\n   639→     * @param readyNodes            The set of ready nodes (to be filled in)\n   640→     * @param unknownLeaderTopics   The set of topics with no leader (to be filled in)\n   641→     * @return The delay for next check\n   642→     */\n   643→    private long partitionReady(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, long nowMs, String topic,\n   644→                                TopicInfo topicInfo,\n   645→                                long nextReadyCheckDelayMs, Set<Node> readyNodes, Set<String> unknownLeaderTopics) {\n   646→        ConcurrentMap<Integer, Deque<ProducerBatch>> batches = topicInfo.batches;\n   647→        // Collect the queue sizes for available partitions to be used in adaptive partitioning.\n   648→        int[] queueSizes = null;\n   649→        int[] partitionIds = null;\n   650→        if (enableAdaptivePartitioning && batches.size() >= metadataSnapshot.cluster().partitionsForTopic(topic).size()) {\n   651→            // We don't do adaptive partitioning until we scheduled at least a batch for all\n   652→            // partitions (i.e. we have the corresponding entries in the batches map), we just\n   653→            // do uniform.  The reason is that we build queue sizes from the batches map,\n   654→            // and if an entry is missing in the batches map, then adaptive partitioning logic\n   655→            // won't know about it and won't switch to it.\n   656→            queueSizes = new int[batches.size()];\n   657→            partitionIds = new int[queueSizes.length];\n   658→        }\n   659→\n   660→        int queueSizesIndex = -1;\n   661→        boolean exhausted = this.free.queued() > 0;\n   662→        for (Map.Entry<Integer, Deque<ProducerBatch>> entry : batches.entrySet()) {\n   663→            TopicPartition part = new TopicPartition(topic, entry.getKey());\n   664→            // Advance queueSizesIndex so that we properly index available\n   665→            // partitions.  Do it here so that it's done for all code paths.\n   666→\n   667→            Node leader = metadataSnapshot.cluster().leaderFor(part);\n   668→            if (leader != null && queueSizes != null) {\n   669→                ++queueSizesIndex;\n   670→                assert queueSizesIndex < queueSizes.length;\n   671→                partitionIds[queueSizesIndex] = part.partition();\n   672→            }\n   673→\n   674→            Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = entry.getValue();\n   675→\n   676→            final long waitedTimeMs;\n   677→            final boolean backingOff;\n   678→            final int backoffAttempts;\n   679→            final int dequeSize;\n   680→            final boolean full;\n   681→\n   682→            OptionalInt leaderEpoch = metadataSnapshot.leaderEpochFor(part);\n   683→\n   684→            // This loop is especially hot with large partition counts. So -\n   685→\n   686→            // 1. We should avoid code that increases synchronization between application thread calling\n   687→            // send(), and background thread running runOnce(), see https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-16226\n   688→\n   689→            // 2. We are careful to only perform the minimum required inside the\n   690→            // synchronized block, as this lock is also used to synchronize producer threads\n   691→            // attempting to append() to a partition/batch.\n   692→\n   693→            synchronized (deque) {\n   694→                // Deques are often empty in this path, esp with large partition counts,\n   695→                // so we exit early if we can.\n   696→                ProducerBatch batch = deque.peekFirst();\n   697→                if (batch == null) {\n   698→                    continue;\n   699→                }\n   700→\n   701→                waitedTimeMs = batch.waitedTimeMs(nowMs);\n   702→                batch.maybeUpdateLeaderEpoch(leaderEpoch);\n   703→                backingOff = shouldBackoff(batch.hasLeaderChangedForTheOngoingRetry(), batch, waitedTimeMs);\n   704→                backoffAttempts = batch.attempts();\n   705→                dequeSize = deque.size();\n   706→                full = dequeSize > 1 || batch.isFull();\n   707→            }\n   708→\n   709→            if (leader == null) {\n   710→                // This is a partition for which leader is not known, but messages are available to send.\n   711→                // Note that entries are currently not removed from batches when deque is empty.\n   712→                unknownLeaderTopics.add(part.topic());\n   713→            } else {\n   714→                if (queueSizes != null)\n   715→                    queueSizes[queueSizesIndex] = dequeSize;\n   716→                if (partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs > 0) {\n   717→                    // Check if we want to exclude the partition from the list of available partitions\n   718→                    // if the broker hasn't responded for some time.\n   719→                    NodeLatencyStats nodeLatencyStats = nodeStats.get(leader.id());\n   720→                    if (nodeLatencyStats != null) {\n   721→                        // NOTE: there is no synchronization between reading metrics,\n   722→                        // so we read ready time first to avoid accidentally marking partition\n   723→                        // unavailable if we read while the metrics are being updated.\n   724→                        long readyTimeMs = nodeLatencyStats.readyTimeMs;\n   725→                        if (readyTimeMs - nodeLatencyStats.drainTimeMs > partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs)\n   726→                            --queueSizesIndex;\n   727→                    }\n   728→                }\n   729→\n   730→                nextReadyCheckDelayMs = batchReady(exhausted, part, leader, waitedTimeMs, backingOff,\n   731→                    backoffAttempts, full, nextReadyCheckDelayMs, readyNodes);\n   732→            }\n   733→        }\n   734→\n   735→        // We've collected the queue sizes for partitions of this topic, now we can calculate\n   736→        // load stats.  NOTE: the stats are calculated in place, modifying the\n   737→        // queueSizes array.\n   738→        topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionLoadStats(queueSizes, partitionIds, queueSizesIndex + 1);\n   739→        return nextReadyCheckDelayMs;\n   740→    }\n   741→\n   742→    /**\n   743→     * Get a list of nodes whose partitions are ready to be sent, and the earliest time at which any non-sendable\n   744→     * partition will be ready; Also return the flag for whether there are any unknown leaders for the accumulated\n   745→     * partition batches.\n   746→     * <p>\n   747→     * A destination node is ready to send data if:\n   748→     * <ol>\n   749→     * <li>There is at least one partition that is not backing off its send\n   750→     * <li><b>and</b> those partitions are not muted (to prevent reordering if\n   751→     *   {@value org.apache.kafka.clients.producer.ProducerConfig#MAX_IN_FLIGHT_REQUESTS_PER_CONNECTION}\n   752→     *   is set to one)</li>\n   753→     * <li><b>and <i>any</i></b> of the following are true</li>\n   754→     * <ul>\n   755→     *     <li>The record set is full</li>\n   756→     *     <li>The record set has sat in the accumulator for at least lingerMs milliseconds</li>\n   757→     *     <li>The accumulator is out of memory and threads are blocking waiting for data (in this case all partitions\n   758→     *     are immediately considered ready).</li>\n   759→     *     <li>The accumulator has been closed</li>\n   760→     * </ul>\n   761→     * </ol>\n   762→     */\n   763→    public ReadyCheckResult ready(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, long nowMs) {\n   764→        Set<Node> readyNodes = new HashSet<>();\n   765→        long nextReadyCheckDelayMs = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n   766→        Set<String> unknownLeaderTopics = new HashSet<>();\n   767→        // Go topic by topic so that we can get queue sizes for partitions in a topic and calculate\n   768→        // cumulative frequency table (used in partitioner).\n   769→        for (Map.Entry<String, TopicInfo> topicInfoEntry : this.topicInfoMap.entrySet()) {\n   770→            final String topic = topicInfoEntry.getKey();\n   771→            nextReadyCheckDelayMs = partitionReady(metadataSnapshot, nowMs, topic, topicInfoEntry.getValue(), nextReadyCheckDelayMs, readyNodes, unknownLeaderTopics);\n   772→        }\n   773→        return new ReadyCheckResult(readyNodes, nextReadyCheckDelayMs, unknownLeaderTopics);\n   774→    }\n   775→\n   776→    /**\n   777→     * Check whether there are any batches which haven't been drained\n   778→     */\n   779→    public boolean hasUndrained() {\n   780→        for (TopicInfo topicInfo : topicInfoMap.values()) {\n   781→            for (Deque<ProducerBatch> deque : topicInfo.batches.values()) {\n   782→                synchronized (deque) {\n   783→                    if (!deque.isEmpty())\n   784→                        return true;\n   785→                }\n   786→            }\n   787→        }\n   788→        return false;\n   789→    }\n   790→\n   791→    private boolean shouldBackoff(boolean hasLeaderChanged, final ProducerBatch batch, final long waitedTimeMs) {\n   792→        boolean shouldWaitMore = batch.attempts() > 0 && waitedTimeMs < retryBackoff.backoff(batch.attempts() - 1);\n   793→        boolean shouldBackoff = !hasLeaderChanged && shouldWaitMore;\n   794→        if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\n   795→            if (shouldBackoff) {\n   796→                log.trace(\n   797→                    \"For {}, will backoff\", batch);\n   798→            } else {\n   799→                log.trace(\n   800→                    \"For {}, will not backoff, shouldWaitMore {}, hasLeaderChanged {}\", batch,\n   801→                    shouldWaitMore, hasLeaderChanged);\n   802→            }\n   803→        } else if (log.isDebugEnabled() && hasLeaderChanged) {\n   804→            // Add less-verbose log at DEBUG.\n   805→            log.debug(\"For {}, leader has changed, hence skipping backoff.\", batch);\n   806→        }\n   807→        return shouldBackoff;\n   808→    }\n   809→\n   810→    private boolean shouldStopDrainBatchesForPartition(ProducerBatch first, TopicPartition tp) {\n   811→        ProducerIdAndEpoch producerIdAndEpoch;\n   812→        if (transactionManager != null) {\n   813→            if (!transactionManager.isSendToPartitionAllowed(tp))\n   814→                return true;\n   815→\n   816→            producerIdAndEpoch = transactionManager.producerIdAndEpoch();\n   817→            if (!producerIdAndEpoch.isValid())\n   818→                // we cannot send the batch until we have refreshed the producer id\n   819→                return true;\n   820→\n   821→            if (!first.hasSequence()) {\n   822→                if (transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(tp) && transactionManager.hasStaleProducerIdAndEpoch(tp)) {\n   823→                    // Don't drain any new batches while the partition has in-flight batches with a different epoch\n   824→                    // and/or producer ID. Otherwise, a batch with a new epoch and sequence number\n   825→                    // 0 could be written before earlier batches complete, which would cause out of sequence errors\n   826→                    return true;\n   827→                }\n   828→\n   829→                if (transactionManager.hasUnresolvedSequence(first.topicPartition))\n   830→                    // Don't drain any new batches while the state of previous sequence numbers\n   831→                    // is unknown. The previous batches would be unknown if they were aborted\n   832→                    // on the client after being sent to the broker at least once.\n   833→                    return true;\n   834→            }\n   835→\n   836→            int firstInFlightSequence = transactionManager.firstInFlightSequence(first.topicPartition);\n   837→            // If the queued batch already has an assigned sequence, then it is being retried.\n   838→            // In this case, we wait until the next immediate batch is ready and drain that.\n   839→            // We only move on when the next in line batch is complete (either successfully or due to\n   840→            // a fatal broker error). This effectively reduces our in flight request count to 1.\n   841→            return firstInFlightSequence != RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE && first.hasSequence()\n   842→                    && first.baseSequence() != firstInFlightSequence;\n   843→        }\n   844→        return false;\n   845→    }\n   846→\n   847→    private List<ProducerBatch> drainBatchesForOneNode(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, Node node, int maxSize, long now) {\n   848→        int size = 0;\n   849→        List<PartitionInfo> parts = metadataSnapshot.cluster().partitionsForNode(node.id());\n   850→        List<ProducerBatch> ready = new ArrayList<>();\n   851→        if (parts.isEmpty())\n   852→            return ready;\n   853→        /* to make starvation less likely each node has it's own drainIndex */\n   854→        int drainIndex = getDrainIndex(node.idString());\n   855→        int start = drainIndex = drainIndex % parts.size();\n   856→        do {\n   857→            PartitionInfo part = parts.get(drainIndex);\n   858→\n   859→            TopicPartition tp = new TopicPartition(part.topic(), part.partition());\n   860→            updateDrainIndex(node.idString(), drainIndex);\n   861→            drainIndex = (drainIndex + 1) % parts.size();\n   862→            // Only proceed if the partition has no in-flight batches.\n   863→            if (isMuted(tp))\n   864→                continue;\n   865→            Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = getDeque(tp);\n   866→            if (deque == null)\n   867→                continue;\n   868→\n   869→            OptionalInt leaderEpoch = metadataSnapshot.leaderEpochFor(tp);\n   870→\n   871→            final ProducerBatch batch;\n   872→            synchronized (deque) {\n   873→                // invariant: !isMuted(tp,now) && deque != null\n   874→                ProducerBatch first = deque.peekFirst();\n   875→                if (first == null)\n   876→                    continue;\n   877→\n   878→                // first != null\n   879→                // Only drain the batch if it is not during backoff period.\n   880→                first.maybeUpdateLeaderEpoch(leaderEpoch);\n   881→                if (shouldBackoff(first.hasLeaderChangedForTheOngoingRetry(), first, first.waitedTimeMs(now)))\n   882→                    continue;\n   883→\n   884→                if (size + first.estimatedSizeInBytes() > maxSize && !ready.isEmpty()) {\n   885→                    // there is a rare case that a single batch size is larger than the request size due to\n   886→                    // compression; in this case we will still eventually send this batch in a single request\n   887→                    break;\n   888→                } else {\n   889→                    if (shouldStopDrainBatchesForPartition(first, tp))\n   890→                        break;\n   891→                }\n   892→\n   893→                batch = deque.pollFirst();\n   894→\n   895→                boolean isTransactional = transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isTransactional();\n   896→                ProducerIdAndEpoch producerIdAndEpoch =\n   897→                    transactionManager != null ? transactionManager.producerIdAndEpoch() : null;\n   898→                if (producerIdAndEpoch != null && !batch.hasSequence()) {\n   899→                    // If the producer id/epoch of the partition do not match the latest one\n   900→                    // of the producer, we update it and reset the sequence. This should be\n   901→                    // only done when all its in-flight batches have completed. This is guarantee\n   902→                    // in `shouldStopDrainBatchesForPartition`.\n   903→                    transactionManager.maybeUpdateProducerIdAndEpoch(batch.topicPartition);\n   904→\n   905→                    // If the batch already has an assigned sequence, then we should not change the producer id and\n   906→                    // sequence number, since this may introduce duplicates. In particular, the previous attempt\n   907→                    // may actually have been accepted, and if we change the producer id and sequence here, this\n   908→                    // attempt will also be accepted, causing a duplicate.\n   909→                    //\n   910→                    // Additionally, we update the next sequence number bound for the partition, and also have\n   911→                    // the transaction manager track the batch so as to ensure that sequence ordering is maintained\n   912→                    // even if we receive out of order responses.\n   913→                    batch.setProducerState(producerIdAndEpoch, transactionManager.sequenceNumber(batch.topicPartition), isTransactional);\n   914→                    transactionManager.incrementSequenceNumber(batch.topicPartition, batch.recordCount);\n   915→                    log.debug(\"Assigned producerId {} and producerEpoch {} to batch with base sequence \" +\n   916→                            \"{} being sent to partition {}\", producerIdAndEpoch.producerId,\n   917→                        producerIdAndEpoch.epoch, batch.baseSequence(), tp);\n   918→\n   919→                    transactionManager.addInFlightBatch(batch);\n   920→                }\n   921→            }\n   922→\n   923→            // the rest of the work by processing outside the lock\n   924→            // close() is particularly expensive\n   925→            batch.close();\n   926→            size += batch.records().sizeInBytes();\n   927→            ready.add(batch);\n   928→\n   929→            batch.drained(now);\n   930→        } while (start != drainIndex);\n   931→        return ready;\n   932→    }\n   933→\n   934→    private int getDrainIndex(String idString) {\n   935→        return nodesDrainIndex.computeIfAbsent(idString, s -> 0);\n   936→    }\n   937→\n   938→    private void updateDrainIndex(String idString, int drainIndex) {\n   939→        nodesDrainIndex.put(idString, drainIndex);\n   940→    }\n   941→\n   942→    /**\n   943→     * Drain all the data for the given nodes and collate them into a list of batches that will fit\n   944→     * within the specified size on a per-node basis. This method attempts to avoid choosing the same\n   945→     * topic-node over and over.\n   946→     *\n   947→     * @param metadataSnapshot  The current cluster metadata\n   948→     * @param nodes             The list of node to drain\n   949→     * @param maxSize           The maximum number of bytes to drain\n   950→     * @param now               The current unix time in milliseconds\n   951→     * @return A list of {@link ProducerBatch} for each node specified with total size less than the\n   952→     * requested maxSize.\n   953→     */\n   954→    public Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> drain(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, Set<Node> nodes, int maxSize, long now) {\n   955→        if (nodes.isEmpty())\n   956→            return Collections.emptyMap();\n   957→\n   958→        Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = new HashMap<>();\n   959→        for (Node node : nodes) {\n   960→            List<ProducerBatch> ready = drainBatchesForOneNode(metadataSnapshot, node, maxSize, now);\n   961→            batches.put(node.id(), ready);\n   962→        }\n   963→        return batches;\n   964→    }\n   965→\n   966→    public void updateNodeLatencyStats(Integer nodeId, long nowMs, boolean canDrain) {\n   967→        // Don't bother with updating stats if the feature is turned off.\n   968→        if (partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs <= 0)\n   969→            return;\n   970→\n   971→        // When the sender gets a node (returned by the ready() function) that has data to send\n   972→        // but the node is not ready (and so we cannot drain the data), we only update the\n   973→        // ready time, then the difference would reflect for how long a node wasn't ready\n   974→        // to send the data.  Then we can temporarily remove partitions that are handled by the\n   975→        // node from the list of available partitions so that the partitioner wouldn't pick\n   976→        // this partition.\n   977→        // NOTE: there is no synchronization for metric updates, so drainTimeMs is updated\n   978→        // first to avoid accidentally marking a partition unavailable if the reader gets\n   979→        // values between updates.\n   980→        NodeLatencyStats nodeLatencyStats = nodeStats.computeIfAbsent(nodeId, id -> new NodeLatencyStats(nowMs));\n   981→        if (canDrain)\n   982→            nodeLatencyStats.drainTimeMs = nowMs;\n   983→        nodeLatencyStats.readyTimeMs = nowMs;\n   984→    }\n   985→\n   986→    /* Visible for testing */\n   987→    public NodeLatencyStats getNodeLatencyStats(Integer nodeId) {\n   988→        return nodeStats.get(nodeId);\n   989→    }\n   990→\n   991→    /* Visible for testing */\n   992→    public BuiltInPartitioner getBuiltInPartitioner(String topic) {\n   993→        return topicInfoMap.get(topic).builtInPartitioner;\n   994→    }\n   995→\n   996→    /**\n   997→     * The earliest absolute time a batch will expire (in milliseconds)\n   998→     */\n   999→    public long nextExpiryTimeMs() {\n  1000→        return this.nextBatchExpiryTimeMs;\n  1001→    }\n  1002→\n  1003→      /* Visible for testing */\n  1004→    public Deque<ProducerBatch> getDeque(TopicPartition tp) {\n  1005→        TopicInfo topicInfo = topicInfoMap.get(tp.topic());\n  1006→        if (topicInfo == null)\n  1007→            return null;\n  1008→        return topicInfo.batches.get(tp.partition());\n  1009→    }\n  1010→\n  1011→    /**\n  1012→     * Get the deque for the given topic-partition, creating it if necessary.\n  1013→     */\n  1014→    private Deque<ProducerBatch> getOrCreateDeque(TopicPartition tp) {\n  1015→        TopicInfo topicInfo = topicInfo.batches.computeIfAbsent(tp.partition(), k -> new ArrayDeque<>());\n  1018→    }\n  1019→\n  1020→    BuiltInPartitioner createBuiltInPartitioner(LogContext logContext, String topic, int stickyBatchSize) {\n  1021→        return new BuiltInPartitioner(logContext, topic, stickyBatchSize);\n  1022→    }\n  1023→\n  1024→    /**\n  1025→     * Deallocate the record batch\n  1026→     */\n  1027→    public void deallocate(ProducerBatch batch) {\n  1028→        incomplete.remove(batch);\n  1029→        // Only deallocate the batch if it is not a split batch because split batch are allocated outside the\n  1030→        // buffer pool.\n  1031→        if (!batch.isSplitBatch())\n  1032→            free.deallocate(batch.buffer(), batch.initialCapacity());\n  1033→    }\n  1034→\n  1035→    /**\n  1036→     * Package private for unit test. Get the buffer pool remaining size in bytes.\n  1037→     */\n  1038→    long bufferPoolAvailableMemory() {\n  1039→        return free.availableMemory();\n  1040→    }\n  1041→\n  1042→    /**\n  1043→     * Are there any threads currently waiting on a flush?\n  1044→     *\n  1045→     * package private for test\n  1046→     */\n  1047→    boolean flushInProgress() {\n  1048→        return flushesInProgress.get() > 0;\n  1049→    }\n  1050→\n  1051→    /**\n  1052→     * Initiate the flushing of data from the accumulator...this makes all requests immediately ready\n  1053→     */\n  1054→    public void beginFlush() {\n  1055→        this.flushesInProgress.getAndIncrement();\n  1056→    }\n  1057→\n  1058→    /**\n  1059→     * Are there any threads currently appending messages?\n  1060→     */\n  1061→    private boolean appendsInProgress() {\n  1062→        return appendsInProgress.get() > 0;\n  1063→    }\n  1064→\n  1065→    /**\n  1066→     * Mark all partitions as ready to send and block until the send is complete\n  1067→     */\n  1068→    public void awaitFlushCompletion() throws InterruptedException {\n  1069→        try {\n  1070→            // Obtain a copy of all of the incomplete ProduceRequestResult(s) at the time of the flush.\n  1071→            // We must be careful not to hold a reference to the ProduceBatch(s) so that garbage\n  1072→            // collection can occur on the contents.\n  1073→            // The sender will remove ProducerBatch(s) from the original incomplete collection.\n  1074→            //\n  1075→            // We use awaitAllDependents() here instead of await() to ensure that if any batch\n  1076→            // was split into multiple batches, we wait for all the split batches to complete.\n  1077→            // This is required to guarantee that all records sent before flush()\n  1078→            // must be fully complete, including records in split batches.\n  1079→            for (ProduceRequestResult result : this.incomplete.requestResults())\n  1080→                result.awaitAllDependents();\n  1081→        } finally {\n  1082→            this.flushesInProgress.decrementAndGet();\n  1083→        }\n  1084→    }\n  1085→\n  1086→    /**\n  1087→     * Check whether there are any pending batches (whether sent or unsent).\n  1088→     */\n  1089→    public boolean hasIncomplete() {\n  1090→        return !this.incomplete.isEmpty();\n  1091→    }\n  1092→\n  1093→    /**\n  1094→     * This function is only called when sender is closed forcefully. It will fail all the\n  1095→     * incomplete batches and return.\n  1096→     */\n  1097→    public void abortIncompleteBatches() {\n  1098→        // We need to keep aborting the incomplete batch until no thread is trying to append to\n  1099→        // 1. Avoid losing batches.\n  1100→        // 2. Free up memory in case appending threads are blocked on buffer full.\n  1101→        // This is a tight loop but should be able to get through very quickly.\n  1102→        do {\n  1103→            abortBatches();\n  1104→        } while (appendsInProgress());\n  1105→        // After this point, no thread will append any messages because they will see the close\n  1106→        // flag set. We need to do the last abort after no thread was appending in case there was a new\n  1107→        // batch appended by the last appending thread.\n  1108→        abortBatches();\n  1109→        this.topicInfoMap.clear();\n  1110→    }\n  1111→\n  1112→    /**\n  1113→     * Go through incomplete batches and abort them.\n  1114→     */\n  1115→    private void abortBatches() {\n  1116→        abortBatches(new KafkaException(\"Producer is closed forcefully.\"));\n  1117→    }\n  1118→\n  1119→    /**\n  1120→     * Abort all incomplete batches (whether they have been sent or not)\n  1121→     */\n  1122→    void abortBatches(final RuntimeException reason) {\n  1123→        for (ProducerBatch batch : incomplete.copyAll()) {\n  1124→            Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = getDeque(batch.topicPartition);\n  1125→            synchronized (dq) {\n  1126→                batch.abortRecordAppends();\n  1127→                dq.remove(batch);\n  1128→            }\n  1129→            batch.abort(reason);\n  1130→            deallocate(batch);\n  1131→        }\n  1132→    }\n  1133→\n  1134→    /**\n  1135→     * Abort any batches which have not been drained\n  1136→     */\n  1137→    void abortUndrainedBatches(RuntimeException reason) {\n  1138→        for (ProducerBatch batch : incomplete.copyAll()) {\n  1139→            Deque<ProducerBatch> dq =
